_CREA (I) _Members Day_

Jain Heights is a sponsor. There is a Plotted Pre Launch. 
Only for CREA (I) Members. Along with Members Day.

So what's special ? Why should a Member feel the necessity to mandatorily attend ? Should we attend even if we don't sell Plots or don't sell Yelhanka ? Also on Tuesday 28th could be an occassion, a client visit, an inspection or just the regular Tuesday Real Estate Holiday for some. So why attend ?

Many answers to that. But presenting only One. 
Are you a CREA (I) *Member* ? 
A Proud CREA (I) *Member*
Then remember it is a *Members* Day.
Not a Committee Day, Association Day, Another Event Day or Just another Day.
Its *Members Day*
For the Members, Of the Members, By the Members.

You have a full day on Monday to reschedule and ensure you block 10 am to 2 pm on Tuesday for the Members Day and help build your own fraternity, business and association. 

The only reason to miss the Event could be an unavoidable Medical Exigency in the family. The rest is Mindset.

What's your Mindset, this Members Day, dear CREA (I) Member ? ðŸ™
